# Mods Removed: 
> * CreativeCore
> * GTNH-Intergalactic
> * Hardcore Darkness
> * MX-Random
> * MouseTweaks
> * ThaumicInventoryScanning
> * Travellers Gear
> * TravellersGearNeo
> * inventory-tweaks
